1)  
The Day of God and the Mission of the Unification Church  
<Prayer> Today, as we welcome this new morning, may Your loving hand be upon countless people, countless nations, and the people of the Republic of Korea, as well as our families. Also, bless us so that we may participate in the world of glory, and have compassion on Your children gathered here to celebrate this day. Bless this day with Your infinite grace.  
Father, today marks the third anniversary of the proclamation of the Day of God. We believe that we alone are commemorating such a day on this earth. We sincerely thank You for allowing us to welcome this unprecedented holy feast in history and to praise Your glory.  
Now, we gather our meager sincerity to commemorate this day and offer it as a glorious day before You, so please accept it. We earnestly hope and wish that this glory experienced by those who attend this day may be cherished and passed down to our descendants for generations to come.  
At this time, bless Your children who are looking toward this place from all over the nation and the countless Your children scattered across the world. Bless them based on the many spirits in the spirit world who have labored for us, Father. We earnestly wish and hope that we may become one world, one family. Also, may all things and all humanity be empowered to assert themselves with autonomous authority.  
We entrust our inadequate hearts to You, Father, so please personally oversee them. Bless us on this day and throughout this year, so that all our plans may flourish and prosper. We earnestly hope and wish that the final front line of victory and unity may expand from ourselves through our families to our nation, country, and world, Father.  
We thank You for accepting everything as Your holy grace and pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.  
<Words> As you know, the 'Day of God' has been commemorated only by our Unification Church until now. However, it goes without saying that this day should not be limited to a commemoration by the Unification Church alone. Therefore, we are in a position where we must fulfill our responsibilities with all our efforts until this nation, this people, and all humanity can jointly celebrate and commemorate this Day of God.  
The Restoration History to Find the Lost Day  
If the ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve, had not fallen and had established a family, the day they formed that family would have been the day of the completion of God's ideal of creation and the day of God's joy. Moreover, it would have been the day when the love relationship between God and humanity was finally established on this earth. That day would have marked the beginning of Adam and Eve as true parents, and it would not only have been a day of joy for humanity but also a day of joy for all creation.  
However, due to the fall of our ancestors, humanity lost the ideal day that God had longed for, the true day that humanity had awaited, and the true day that all creation had awaited. The purpose of the providence of salvation and restoration is to find all these lost days again.  
How do we restore them? We must go back by taking all things as conditions. Therefore, until now, the conditions we could offer before God have not been people but all things. We have been offering all things as sacrifices. From there, we have been seeking to find a person who can become one with the sacrifice. This history has been unfolding from the Old Testament era through the New Testament era centered on Christianity. In this history, the one who came to this earth as a global entity that could become one with the sacrifice is none other than Jesus.  
Jesus came as the embodiment of the sacrifice, and thus He is the central being who can govern all sacrifices. Furthermore, Jesus came to play an intermediary role, directly controlling material sacrifices so that humanity could establish a relationship with God. However, because the Israelite nation and Judaism could not accept Him, Jesus was unable to fulfill that mission and passed away.  
To offer a sacrifice, there must be a people and a nation. Therefore, Jesus had to represent humanity and offer a victorious sacrifice, not a dead one, before God, as a resurrected entity. In doing so, the embodiment of that sacrifice, Jesus, had to escape the conditions of accusation from Satan. The conditions for Satan to accuse must not be established. If a sacrifice is offered incorrectly, Satan will accuse.  
Since the sacrifice is the condition to separate God and Satan, if it is offered incorrectly, it results in giving it to Satan, while if it is offered correctly, it results in being dedicated to God. Thus, until Jesus, there was no history of offering sacrifices before God, but centered on Jesus, that historical era had to be transcended.  
By binding the sacrifice and establishing a foundation of complete victory, a society centered on Jesus had to be formed, one that only God could govern and where Satan could neither accuse nor intervene. Nevertheless, because the Israelite nation and state could not uphold Jesus, they lost that foundation. Therefore, centered on Christianity, this has been reorganized to develop globally.  
However, this is not about laying the foundation of the first Israel. In other words, Christianity did not develop as a specific religion that leads a particular nation or people. Nor did it develop while completely destroying the earthly foundation and looking toward a nation to be established in the spiritual world. It has been developing while longing for the nation of hope, the Kingdom of Heaven.  
This spiritual development does not aim to form a national organization but rather to develop individuals who can form such a national organization. This has been the history of Christianity until now. Thus, we must establish the Second Israel that can achieve the purpose of individual salvation, and we must offer a victorious sacrifice before God by organizing a new nation and a new people on this earth. We know that history has gone through this path of indemnity.  
What the Unification Church Proposes  
So what does our Unification Church propose today? It is to establish a realm of authority where Satan cannot accuse, having passed through the age of all things as sacrifices and the age of sons and daughters as sacrifices. Thus, we must prepare a victorious sacrifice, that is, a resurrected entity, so that God can freely take and govern it at any time. This is the purpose of the restoration providence until now.  
Such sons and daughters must be manifested on this earth. This is both the thought of the Second Advent and the thought of True Parents. Therefore, for True Parents to be manifested on this earth, they must go through the sacrificial process. In other words, the Old Testament era must go through the process of all things as sacrifices, the New Testament era must go through the process of children as sacrifices, and the Era of the Completed Testament must go through the process of parents as sacrifices.  
When offering a sacrifice, it must be offered in such a way that God can fully accept it, overcoming the conditions for accusation as a parent. Thus, centered on that parent, we must create the authority for God to govern the horizontal world freely and to command and lead as He wishes. That is the family. That family becomes the origin from which a nation can emerge and a people can begin. When that happens, the ideology of a new heaven can be realized from there.  
By establishing the relationship of True Parents of humanity that can be completed in this way, God's love intervenes in these True Parents, and all things are connected. Therefore, heaven can concentrate on Adam and Eve, and all things can also concentrate. In other words, through Adam and Eve, heaven and earth can be connected. Here, the angelic world and the spirit world are certainly to cooperate, not oppose. However, until now, the reality of the sacrifice has been in conflict both in heaven and on earth. Therefore, we have been working to connect heaven to earth, centering on people, and to achieve unity, and also to achieve unity between all things centered on this person.  
Thus far, we have been working to achieve unity with all things through sacrifices, but ultimately, it is not all things themselves that can achieve unity, but rather it is humanity. Without people being the center, there can be no connection to heaven. This is the original standard. The one who came to restore this standard is Jesus and the Holy Spirit. However, while Jesus and the Holy Spirit established this standard spiritually, they could not become the center that could connect both spirit and flesh. Therefore, to complete this standard in both spirit and flesh, Christianity has been developing centered on the thought of the Second Advent while looking forward to the time of hope.  
So what mission does the Unification Church bear today? It is not to look forward to the time of hope that Christianity desires, but to bear the mission of going forth centered on the standard of the substantial realization of that hope. What is that standard? True Parents. Those True Parents must be connected to God, to all people on earth, and to the spirit world. In other words, they must be connected to God, to all people on earth, and even to the angelic world. Thus, all beings must establish the authority that God can directly govern centered on True Parents with one purpose. Only then will God's purpose and the work of creation be fulfilled.  
The Historical 1960s  
So when will this be accomplished? It will be achieved when Adam and Eve receive the blessing, that is, through the holy wedding ceremony. When we think about the restoration process that unfolds to achieve this, since the ancestors of humanity fell at the level of completion of the growth stage, today's humanity must rise back to that level. The stage of rebirth corresponds to the age of servants, the growth stage corresponds to the age of adopted children, and the completion stage corresponds to the age of legitimate children.  
In this view, the time of Jacob is the age of servants, and the Old Testament era, which corresponds to the stage of rebirth, is the age of servants. Therefore, through the appearance of Jesus' gospel on this earth, history transitioned to the realm of adopted children.  
Since the ancestors of humanity fell at the level of completion of the growth stage, they must be recreated with the external form and connection of that son to be raised to the position of completion of the growth stage to inherit the legitimate child authority. In other words, because the ancestors of humanity fell at the level of completion of the growth stage, they must reach that level to be restored.  
However, since the fall originated in the family, without establishing the form of this family, one cannot rise to that standard in restoration. Therefore, in the 1960s, centered on the Teacher, the Unification Church transcended that standard. Because they transcended that standard, the 7-year course emerged.  
So what is this 7-year course? It is a period to completely cut off all inner and outer content that has been invaded by Satan until now and to completely defend against Satan. Defense must be carried out personally and at the family level. This realm was the goal of the development of Judaism centered on the nation of Israel and the people of Israel, and both the purpose of the nation of Israel and the purpose of Judaism had to be fulfilled within this realm. However, after Jesus died, there was no longer a point to resolve the purpose of Israel or Judaism within this realm.  
Therefore, Jesus must come again to achieve the purpose within this realm. He must come not as a grown child but as a reborn child. He must come as a reborn child and find a bride. In other words, because the ancestor of humanity, Adam, lost the dominion by listening to Eve, Jesus must come as a complete person who can align with God's love and fulfill the purpose of creation, and He must find a woman who can align with Him. Just as Eve was created through Adam, He must establish Eve, that is, the bride, through the process of recreation to establish a new family, and only then can He ascend toward the world of completion. This time marks the end of the fallen age and the beginning of a new age. Historically, this is the year 1960.  
Entering the year 1960, those who seek the results of the historical transition of the world do not know, but the Unification Church knows. However, it must be understood that this is not motivated by the historical world but rather that the movement of the Unification Church, which God has been promoting, is the motivation. After going through the 7-year course and then the 3-year course, today the world situation has entered a natural environment where we can freely navigate in all directions. This is an inevitable conclusion. Therefore, where should we receive blessings? We must receive them at the level of completion of the growth stage.
Today, the fact that the True Parents have manifested at the center of this earth is not a private matter of heaven. This is where a new True Parents' Day begins. The question of how to return the lost false parents to the position of True Parents has been the desire of humanity and the desire of God until now.

Until the Day of God is proclaimed, before restoring these True Parents, that is, before finding the family of Adam and Eve who did not fall, it is impossible to have unfallen descendants or an unfallen world of creation. Without standing in a position where humans can freely govern the world of creation, God cannot act as God. Therefore, we established Parents' Day, Children's Day, and the Day of All Things centered around the year 1960.

Parents must exist for children to exist, and because of children, we can govern all things. To govern all things, we must be fruitful, multiply, and fill the earth. It is not just Adam and Eve who are meant to govern. Children are the horizontal foundation, and parents are the vertical foundation. That is why parents are in the position of God on earth. With this vertical foundation established, we are meant to govern all things.

Thus, after establishing Parents' Day in the Unification Church, we established Children's Day, and after establishing Children's Day, we established the Day of All Things. These days of Parents and All Things, as well as Children's Day itself, are not within the realm of the fallen rights but are within God's dominion. In other words, they are in a position that is free from Satan's accusation rights. Therefore, we can establish a direct relationship with God.

Based on this standard, by moving from the completion stage of the growth period to the completion stage of the resurrection period, we enter into God's dominion. Only then can we finally restore the original Eden that did not fall. From there, we must walk the seven-year course centered on God, which is the second seven-year course. Here, God's will is fulfilled. That is why, after finishing the first seven-year course in 1967, we proclaimed the Day of God on the first day of the first month in 1968.

That day was the day when the teacher's first seven-year course ended, and it was the day when the internal heart connection of human history was severed between the spiritual and physical worlds. However, since these separations were centered on God, we must determine the representative standard of the whole that can connect to God on the first level. After that, we must work for the nation or the world. Only then can we step beyond all conditions that Satan can accuse and establish a free environment for liberation, creating a condition for restoration to face God. The Unification Church was able to set the Day of God because it established such a family standard.

You cannot imagine how difficult it was to bring forth this Day of God. The day we established God's Day was the hardest.

No matter how much Parents' Day has been established, if there is no Children's Day to support it, Parents' Day cannot fulfill its role as Parents' Day. Likewise, even if Children's Day is established, without establishing the Day of All Things, Children's Day cannot fulfill its responsibility as Children's Day. Therefore, God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and the Day of All Things must completely unite and receive God's dominion. The fact that this has not been achieved until now is the cause of lamentation. The Day of God, proclaimed globally on the first day of the first month in 1968, was established to connect these.

Three years have passed since then. This three-year period is the period that children must take responsibility for. During this time, centered on the heavenly family on earth, we must connect the vertical standard to the horizontal standard, and we must prosper toward the world centered on this nation and this people. We were told to be fruitful and multiply and fill the earth, so today we must carry out a movement to multiply thirty million centered on the Unification tribe on the foundation of the Korean Peninsula. Thus, we must indemnify all historical conditions that Satan can accuse in the north, south, east, and west, establishing a victorious position that has been resurrected in a substantial way, which is the foundation of blessed families. This is what is called the Unification tribe.

Here, this Unification tribe must indemnify and restore the failures of Abraham and all the conditions where many prophets after Adam came forth according to the will but failed, connecting them as substantial objects centered on the family of True Parents to become completely one. Only then can this organization develop. From this perspective, there are areas where blessed families have not taken responsibility until now. Therefore, the new second movement presented this year is a measure to forgive all that those families could not fulfill and to transition to a new world. The reason for commanding the entire participation in this winter witnessing is there.

With the proclamation of this Day of God, the world situation will change drastically from January 1968. In the future, domestic and Asian situations will also experience turmoil at times. Before this turmoil comes to this land, this Asia, we must prepare internally and solidify the internal foundation that can manage that turmoil. This is currently the mission of the Unification Church.

This Day of God was established after the most arduous efforts centered on the historical process. Only when God is pleased and establishes Himself on this earth can the creation also have a foundation of rest. If God cannot establish Himself, there can be no foundation of rest for the creation. Just as a family cannot achieve a happy home centered on parents if the parents' hearts are not at peace, so too, without the authority to sing of happiness in freedom and to establish oneself in a free environment centered on God, who is the Lord of Heaven, can a new order be established in this world.

Then, who moves this world? It is not humans who move it. It is God who moves behind the scenes. He only moves after establishing the authority to do so. Therefore, we must establish the Day of God. Without establishing the Day of God, there is no way to manage this world. The fact that the Unification Church has presented a content that no organization or person has ever thought of in the historical age and proclaimed the Day of God to the world is undoubtedly a great achievement of the Unification Church.

Today, you are here to celebrate this Day of God, to hear this content, to prepare a feast, and to commemorate it as your holiday. You must recognize that this is a glory that no prophet or saint in history, including Jesus, has ever had. As you commemorate the Day of God today, you are in a position to directly face the True Parents and have the qualifications of true children, a position where you can claim and inherit the true world as your own. Standing in a place where you can hear and feel this content through your eyes and senses while alive is an immense grace that no one in the historical age has ever experienced, done, or seen.

Then how much should we celebrate the Day of God? We must celebrate it greater than any day of celebration in history, with all our sincerity, on a national and global scale. Such a day must come. Bringing such a day is the mission of our Unification Church today.

Today, you have welcomed the third Day of God. How should we welcome this three-year course, that is, the first Day of God, the second Day of God, and the third Day of God? We must welcome the second more nationally than the first, and the third more nationally than the second. As the numbers increase, this world must enter into a realm where it can celebrate this day even more greatly, and only then will God's will be fulfilled centered on the world.

Even if you have achieved a personal kingdom today, if you cannot apply that to your family, you cannot determine a stable place where the individual can rest. Likewise, even if you have achieved a family kingdom, without establishing a victorious foundation for the tribal environment, you cannot establish a stable foundation for the family kingdom. Furthermore, to establish a stable position for the tribe, you must determine a foundation centered on the nation, and to lay a foundation where the nation can rest, you must establish a foundation centered on the world. You are in the process of developing in this way.

So, to what extent has our church come today? We have entered into a time when we can cross over to the nation and the world. However, not everyone is like that. If the center centered on God is normal, a new history will develop from there. To use a tree as an analogy, if the roots are normal, the branches will also develop. Even if the trunk is cut off, as long as the roots are alive, new branches can sprout and grow into a large tree over the years, becoming a new tree.

Wise people understand how to celebrate the Day of God in what kind of environment and strive to prepare that environment. In other words, a wise person is someone who can celebrate the Day of God by establishing a family environment rather than someone who celebrates it individually. A person who can celebrate the Day of God by establishing a tribal environment is wiser than anyone else, and such a family is wiser than any other family. Furthermore, a family that can commemorate the Day of God centered on the nation is a blessed family, and a nation that can have a day to celebrate God centered on the state is a wise nation. Thus, when the entire world centered on each nation gathers to participate and celebrate the Day of God, only then will the sovereignty of heaven be established on this earth, and in the near future, this earth will enter into a realm of destiny that can be restored.

To survive in enemy territory

Facing the tremendous issue of national restoration that we desire, let us think from a different angle. Today, when we look at the earth, it resembles a fisherman who has drifted in a storm and landed on shore with a damaged boat, in a position that has nothing to do with God, that is, in the realm where Satan operates. This is how the Unification Church has appeared. The emergence of the Unification Church on this earth is akin to Jesus coming to this earth with the gospel.

Having come to this earth in such a position, from the perspective of the world of Satan, it is the prince of the enemy nation. In other words, it is like a heavenly prince who has landed in the enemy nation of the world of Satan after drifting. Therefore, if Satan knows the reality, he will not leave it alone. He might leave it alone until he knows, but once he knows, he will not leave it alone. He cannot help but engage in a movement to strike it down.

So, what is the way to respond to this? It cannot be done with fists. It cannot be done with power. If you try to do it with power and get occupied, you will become a prisoner. If that happens, you will inevitably have to become a slave of that nation. After paying the price of death, there is no way to revive without going through the process of becoming a slave of that nation. If you do not want to become a slave, you will simply perish.

That is why many of the ancestors who came out with the will of goodness and Jesus, who represented goodness as the fruit of four thousand years of history, faced this kind of fate. Because he came to the land of the enemy, he could not exercise the authority of being a son of God in the enemy nation. Therefore, he had to carry out underground movements to lay the foundation to exercise God's authority. This is why, in the Bible, when Jesus testified that he was the Son of God and also testified that he would come again, he told no one to inform anyone. Thus, he kept it absolutely secret from Rome, the Israelite people, and Judaism. In other words, that era was the era of underground movements, the underground guerrilla era. And Jesus was the leader of the underground guerrilla organization.

Thus, one cannot avoid becoming a slave. One must become a lower slave than the people of that nation. Therefore, one must have conditions that can testify to the needs of that nation and environment and can serve as a fence. Otherwise, one cannot leave a foothold for survival. Therefore, you must understand that our ancestors who came with the will of goodness made every effort to stand on this earth as slaves.

A miracle among miracles

Now, the Unification Church has laid a national foundation and a global foundation after more than ten years of history. Therefore, even if the 600,000 troops of the Republic of Korea are mobilized, they cannot eliminate the Unification Church. The Unification Church will not disappear. When we consider this, what is the difference between the time of Jesus 2,000 years ago and today? Of course, it is an undeniable fact that God has created the authority of democracy through the historical process, establishing a foundation for freedom of the press, freedom of religion, and freedom of assembly, thereby achieving results like today.

If the circumstances had changed and the leader of the Unification Church had initiated a new movement centered on these principles 2,000 years ago during the time of Jesus, all of you following the teacher would have crossed the valley of death. If you had not become sacrificial offerings of martyrdom, you would not have been able to occupy the path to go before God.

Today, although our Unification Church has worked hard over more than ten years, how many people have died fighting in the pioneering areas for the will in the history of the Unification Church? How many have starved to death? There are many incidents in the world where people are beaten to death and starve to death. However, the fact that we have not died in a place where we could have been beaten to death is due to God's love. God's protection has been great. Moreover, the reason we have not starved to death in a position where we could have starved is that God has fed us. The fact that we were in an environment where we could have been beaten to death but did not die, and in a position where we could have starved but did not starve, is because God saved us. This is something you must understand. 

Until now, among the descendants of the enemy, countless people have been crying out...
In an opposing environment, the fact that not a single life has been harmed and not a single person has been sacrificed while laying this foundation is due to the great love of God. How immense and tragic was the history of Christianity paying the price of blood for 400 years centered around the Roman Empire? When comparing that history to the present, we can see that the content of the gospel preached by Jesus in that era and the gospel preached by our Unification Church today is on a different level. In that time, the concepts of God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day were unimaginable. Of course, it is not that Jesus did not know. If he did not know, God would have taught him. It is truly pitiful that Jesus, who came and went in a social environment where he could not even express such words or perform such actions, had to endure that. 

However, the fact that today you can see, hear, and celebrate God's Day with your body, and gather your hearts to welcome God is a historical event. This is a cosmic event, and no matter how great a miracle exists in this world, there is no greater miracle than this. 

Today is the day that God has awaited for 6,000 years, the day when Jesus and the Holy Spirit have traversed the places of bloodshed centered around countless prophets and sages. On this day, we must shed the mask of the entire history where humanity has not been able to stand before God and become a liberated form. To find true sons and daughters who can face God directly and call Him Father without shame, and to establish a family centered on God's love with such sons and daughters, God has worked hard until now, as have Jesus and the Holy Spirit. The countless prophets, sages, and saints who have come and gone throughout history have done the same. Religious people have also worked hard to open the doors in all directions—north, south, east, and west—to globally spread the ideology of hope. 

To see God's Day, we must recognize that the stages of responsible missions differ according to each era. When one stage of mission ends, it is the historical fact that the mission is handed over to the next responsible person who will remain for future generations, leading to a unified ideological world. We never dreamed that the organization that would inherit and clearly convey all the core contents of this providence would be the Unification Church. Now, I have reached a stage where I can speak about this so openly that it can be believed. 

Right after liberation, when 30 million people were rejoicing and celebrating their freedom, God blessed us so that our nation could become one with sovereignty and rejoice in being liberated from oppression. At that time, our nation should have created a social environment to thank God and seek His will. However, we only clamored for the sovereignty of the Republic of Korea and the nation. No one fought to make the Republic of Korea the foundation of heaven and the heavenly nation. Even though we had made all the necessary preparations for that, even the followers of the religion forgot that they should carry out that work under heaven's command and were swept away by the sound of the liberation trumpet. 

In such circumstances, our Unification Church has, through nearly twenty years of history, stood alone and has now entered a realm where it can be recognized as a spiritual organization, a new religion. 

Today, our Unification Church has sustained itself to see God's Day. The reason the teacher has invested his entire life until now is to establish God's Day. This may sound simple, but the content is extremely complex. If we understand the meaning and look at the content of Jesus' time, we see that Jesus was destined to die. He could not avoid death. In the emotional realm, environmental realm, historical realm, and temporal realm, everything was in disarray, and without establishing a foundation to contend with Satan centered on God, we cannot see God's Day. 

How much have you contributed to establishing this God's Day? How much have you contributed to establishing Parents' Day? To Children's Day, and to All Things Day? You have contributed not at all. The only contribution you can claim is that you have taken on the mission of re-establishing the foundation of the 4,000 years of history that the Israelite people lost. Even in connecting this, your cooperation has been lacking. 

That is why the teacher had to connect everything. It is inevitable. Why? Because Adam and Eve, who should have been the true ancestors of humanity, fell and lost God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day. It was because the ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve, made mistakes. Therefore, the one who bears the responsibility to restore this, the one who carries the mission of the true parents that humanity desires, must come and connect it. God's Day must also be established by that person, as must the days of the true parents, true children, and true all things. This is something that no one else can do. 

The privilege that the Unification Church has today, having resolved the grievances over ten years, is nothing short of a great miracle. Among these great achievements, the position where you can directly participate, regard God as your Father, and see the earthly teacher as your True Parent to celebrate such days is different from the unfortunate position during Jesus' time. 

You do not know the value of the Unification Church. Jesus, who lost the familial environment he should have been honored in, and John the Baptist and his group who should have supported him, were rejected. Jesus fell into despair because the environment that Judaism should have revived completely collapsed. You do not realize that Jesus' position and your position are different. 

A person born as a prince does not know his own value. Only by being born as a lowly commoner can one understand the authority and value of a prince. Similarly, because you are within the Unification Church, you do not know how great the value of the Unification Church is. However, spirits in the spiritual world know well. Even the spirits at the lowest level of heaven know well. Of course, those in the center know better than anyone else. 

Likewise, those who understand the connections of the spiritual world today and are devoted in the world of virtue, even if they are not members of the Unification Church, know how precious the Unification Church is. Nevertheless, among the members of the Unification Church, there are many who do not understand that value. Many people, unable to overcome their personal suffering, betray the church and abandon this path to escape their own death. 

To establish this one day, God has walked the path of death. Jesus and the Holy Spirit have also shed tears of blood for this one day. Moreover, countless ancestors in Christianity have paid the price of blood and crossed the peaks of death to find this day. Therefore, this day is the day that encapsulates all the grievances of history. We must become people who can transcend the conditions presented to establish this one day, rather than being those who fall short of those conditions. That is the path we must take. 

To do this, we must unite our hearts and bodies to genuinely celebrate God's Day and stand in a position where we can say, "I am on heaven's side." We must not stand on the side of Satan and act as spies, but rather, we must create a foundation where we can march with God, declaring that if you confront Satan, I will confront him too. Until now, history has fought centered on religion for this purpose. 

So, how should the Unification Church lay this foundation today? We must take the position of a servant. In other words, they are families that have been born by resurrecting the historical conditions of indemnity. That is historical. The teacher's family is a family that has won on that history and temporal foundation, appearing with a victorious authority from a realistic standpoint. 

By completely uniting the teacher's family and the 36 families, they must establish the standards that could not be started in that environment at that time by recovering the past and present of Jesus. 

You yourselves have no way to go in this reality without the teacher's family. Your families have no way to go into a new world in this reality without the teacher's family. You cannot take the lead in going. 

The teacher's family must take the lead centered on the realistic standard. Therefore, you must become a fence and fertilizer from behind, doing everything possible to ensure that the teacher's family can develop. Only then will your families develop.

However, until now, that has not been the case. Until now, the teacher has been in a position to pull your families along. You should have been supporting the teacher's family, but it has been the opposite. The teacher has been in a position to pull you along until now. So, how long should this continue? It should not be like that. Once the indemnity period passes, it does not need to continue.

The Reason for Mobilizing Families

Therefore, as we move into the 1970s, we are once again starting families. It is time for the 36 families to step forward. The 72 families and the 120 families are also preparing for this. You must understand that the teacher has been working hard since entering December 1969, particularly strengthening family gatherings to prepare for this time. 

Because there has been such a tremendous internal purpose, special gatherings have been held until now. So, you must understand that this time, we are mobilizing everyone.

As families that have come with the teacher until now, you must indemnify what you have not been responsible for. It is not enough to just overlook what has not been done. If you have not fulfilled your responsibilities, you must indemnify again in the realistic environment. Your families must eliminate all such environments and step forward to act, which will be the condition of indemnity for that, which is why during this winter vacation, we intend to put women at the forefront.

You must think gratefully about the things that have been done centered on God's tremendous love. This is the position we are currently facing, and we must clearly understand that this is our mission.

By unifying this with the standards that God desires and the standards that Jesus desires, we will have results similar to those of Jesus achieving the purpose of His life through His birth. As we renew this fruition, I hope that you will appear as the substance that Jesus desired, and I emphasized the significance of celebrating the day of Jesus' birth today. Do you understand? "Yes."

<Prayer> Father, how much effort have You made to come to us, who have been foolish since the fall of humanity? We feel ashamed.

No matter how inadequate, lacking, or unfulfilled the family that You have established until now may be, when we think of the fact that You have led this tremendous historical story into a realistic family of resurrection, we must be sons and daughters who feel that even a million thanks are not enough.

Let this family become the fence of the family that the Father desires and become the factor of all development, and let us clearly understand that unless this is connected through history to reality, a new world cannot emerge.

From now on, we must respect the 36 families, 72 families, and 120 families. In order to manifest the glory of historical resurrection, to manifest the glory of era resurrection, and to lay the foundation to manifest the glory of hopeful resurrection in the future, we sincerely hope and wish to become sons and daughters who can truly appreciate the fact that You have established families.

The 72 families have lived without knowing the position of the 36 families. The 120 families have lived without knowing the position of the 72 families, and the 430 families have lived without knowing the position of the 120 families. 

Now, we must establish a new family tradition and live accordingly. As we approach the new morning of the 1970s, I earnestly ask and wish that this time may be a time of adorning the holy day of Jesus' birth and making new promises and new resolutions. 

Because of today, may you be pleased, and because of today, may we be equipped with a foundation of internal and external victory that allows us to recognize ourselves without shame as we welcome tomorrow. I earnestly ask this, and I have offered all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 

3) 
May the Will be fulfilled 

We know that both the Father in heaven and the people living on earth have not yet fulfilled the Will, and history continues to flow. However, you all know well that the reason this Will has not been fulfilled is not because of God, but because of us humans. In other words, it is because Adam and Eve fell that this Will has failed. 

Therefore, we understand that God has been working hard to restore this failed Will to fulfill it as originally intended, and this has been the historical process and providential course until now. 

However, for this Will to be realized, there must be people who can fulfill it. God has chosen people who can uphold the Will through the long historical ages, starting from the family of Adam, to the families of Noah, Abraham, Moses, and Joseph. If the person chosen cannot connect the heavenly relationship to the earth, then even the direction to fulfill the Will cannot be established. We have learned this well through the providential course. 

When we look at our Unification Church today, the question is whether we can fulfill this Will or not as we move forward with the Will in mind on the early morning of January 4, 1970, at the former headquarters church. 

The Will pertains to individuals as well as to the whole, so without people who can address the Will pertaining to individuals and those who can address the Will pertaining to the whole, the Will cannot be fulfilled. Even if the time for the Will to be fulfilled has come, if that person does not carry out their responsibilities, they will lose even the moment when the Will can be fulfilled. 

Conditions necessary to fulfill the Will 

To fulfill the Will, people are absolutely necessary, and then the timing becomes an issue. Timing is always a matter of concern. At the same time, there must be conditions that can fulfill the Will related to both time and people. 

From this perspective, I will speak under the title "May the Will be fulfilled!" 

How long has humanity awaited this throughout the long historical process? Today, it is not only us who await this; countless people throughout the historical ages who have pursued goodness and stood on God's side in opposition to the evil world have all had the heart that says, "May the Will be fulfilled!" 

However, the time when the Will has been fulfilled has not yet come. Many people have come and gone trying to fulfill the Will, but the person who can completely realize the purpose of the Will and make it either heavenly or for humanity has not yet appeared on this earth. 

The Unification Church has manifested around this tremendous historical task. Therefore, all current members of the Unification Church, as well as countless people who will come in the future, should hope for the fulfillment of the Will. We must recognize that this is the task that lies before us. 

From this perspective, we in the Unification Church today must not be like the countless prophets who have come and gone while centering on the Will until now. If we become like those who were swept away by the circumstances of their times and failed to fulfill the Will, then it will be impossible to fulfill the Will at this point in time. 

So what should we do? We must be superior in every aspect of addressing the Will today compared to the countless people who tried to address the Will in the past. In terms of our attitude towards the Will and our lifestyle, we must place a superior self before the Will, or it will be impossible to fulfill it. 

When we look at individuals, what is the difference between people of the past and people today? People are all the same. However, the people of the past lived in simpler circumstances, such as their living environments, world situations, or various social systems. In contrast, we live in a complicated world. We must recognize that we are in a distracted environment. 

When we consider the environment of the past, where people addressed the Will with single-minded devotion, they were not necessarily above us today. They devoted their full efforts to the Will from a simple position, but they could not achieve it. Therefore, we must understand that in our distracted environment today, it is impossible to fulfill the Will without double the effort and double the loyalty compared to them. 

To fulfill the Will, we must possess a heart greater than that of Jesus and put in sincere effort. Among the people of the past, there was no one who thought they could fulfill the Will alone. To fulfill the Will, they always sought God's cooperation. The more inadequate they felt, the more they sought God's cooperation, which is an undeniable fact. 

Similarly, we ourselves are seeking God's cooperation to fulfill this Will. Therefore, in seeking cooperation, we must double our sincerity compared to the people of the past. In other words, if the people of the past put in a hundred percent of their sincerity, we must put in a million or ten million percent of our sincerity. We cannot overlook the issue that without possessing superior internal and external qualities compared to them, fulfilling the Will will be impossible. 

Many prophets and sages have come and gone throughout history, but among them, Jesus Christ came to this earth as the Son of God. After living for over 30 years, at the final moment heading towards the cross, he prayed, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will." (Matthew 26:39). We must conclude that we cannot be inferior to the emotional standard he had at that serious moment of prayer. 

So what must be different in the way we approach God the Father today compared to how Jesus approached Him? Our internal emotional state in approaching God must be different from Jesus' internal emotional state. In other words, we must have a connection that allows our feelings to be superior to those of Jesus living in this era; this is an unavoidable conclusion. 

So do I possess the heart that Jesus had when he earnestly prayed before God in the Garden of Gethsemane? This is an issue that cannot be overlooked. Next, we must consider the position in which Jesus prayed. Jesus did not pray out of fear of his impending death. He prayed because he was in a position where he would lose the nation and people of Israel that God had come to find. We must understand the sad and dire circumstances that led Jesus to pray in such a way. He was in an extreme position from which he could not turn back. 

Today, we must have an attitude towards the issues of our nation, our people, and even the world that surpasses our own nationality. We must recognize this as a mission we must carry out and a historical responsibility we must shoulder. Thus, I must reach a position that surpasses the emotional connection of Jesus. This is the issue at hand. 

"May the Will be fulfilled! May your will be done, Father." Here, the wish remains for the future. To bridge the gap between the present and the future, we must walk the path of indemnity that pays the price of blood and the path of death through the cross. We must recognize that there are pits that cannot be filled without doing so. In facing this tremendous Will in our time, the question is how we can embody the heart that Jesus had while praying in the Garden of Gethsemane. 

Considering God's 4,000-year providential history concerning Israel, how serious must Jesus have felt knowing that if Israel lost itself, its fate would decline and God's blessings would shift to the Gentiles? We must become individuals who surpass the serious heart of Jesus who struggled in such a serious position. Otherwise, we are far too inadequate to fulfill the path of indemnity that Jesus walked while saying, "May the Will be fulfilled." Therefore, it is a matter of becoming a true person who can fulfill the Will. 

God's Will and Our Attitude 

When you center your work on the Will and move forward with the heart of "May the Will be fulfilled," it is not about your individual fulfillment. In saying "fulfill it," the subject is God, and we are in a relative position. We must be in a relative position that can unite with that subject. However, since the Will must be fulfilled through the union of God and us, fulfilling this Will is God's demand and the mission that remains for us. 

When we consider how to connect God's Will with our mission, it cannot be done with just individuals. The internal heart that Jesus had when he prayed, "May your will be done, Father," while facing the cross must also be present in us today. 

The individual Will and God's Will are different. When viewed from the perspective of individuals, each person is in different circumstances. Since the circumstances they are in, their historical backgrounds, and the environmental conditions of their times are all different, they have their own convictions based on those differences. However, these individual wills cannot harmonize with God's Will centered on the overall restoration providence. The more diverse the contents, the lower the probability of fulfilling the Will becomes. 

In this regard, we who must fulfill the Will should disregard all factors centered on our individual wills and express the overall factors centered on God in our lives. The issue is how to establish a personal standard that can express the entire character of heaven centered on oneself. 

Therefore, we must have the mindset that I was born for the Will, I live for the Will, and I cannot demand anything else. In other words, we must always keep within our sphere of life the position where we can negotiate with the conditions of prayer that Jesus had when he said, "Father, not my will, but yours be done." Thus, I must stand in a position where I can fulfill the Will, saying, "Father, who governs the Will, please guide and command me regarding the Will." 

How to develop that position within my sphere of life and my life course is the most important issue for us who stand in the position of fulfilling the Will, isn't it? 

"Not my will, but yours be done." Here, there can be no personal will. There can be no trace of my will whatsoever. You must understand this. When God's Will is fulfilled, my will is completed as a whole. My individual will can only be fulfilled within the limits of the national rights if I am a citizen. If I am a nation, it is difficult to transcend the limits of fulfilling the Will within the national rights. Similarly, if I am part of this world, it is difficult to surpass the limits of fulfilling the Will in this world. 

However, the Will centered on the Father transcends historicality. Because it is a Will that transcends time and space, a person standing within that Will is already in a position where their own will has been fulfilled. This is how it works. My will stands in a position that has already been fulfilled. 

Then what is my original will? My will must be something that is born from heaven, lives from heaven, and can receive purpose from heaven. We must be able to stand in a position where we have fulfilled the Will without needing to negotiate in prayer. From this perspective, we must discover ourselves who can transcend the conditions that Jesus had while praying in the Garden of Gethsemane, and we must find ourselves who can endure through that Will. Thus, we must have a sense of awareness and subjectivity that we have been set before the Will. How to embody this is an important issue. 

Timing is crucial 

However, even if one has become such a person, if the time to fulfill the Will has not come, the Will will not be fulfilled. No matter how capable a person is to fulfill the Will, if the time is not right, it cannot be fulfilled. Just as there are morning, noon, evening, and night in a day, there are also specific times in the process of fulfilling the Will. The timing must not be reversed. 

No matter how excellent a person may be in fulfilling the Will, if they do not properly align with the timing, they will not be able to fulfill it. Why was Jesus unable to fulfill the Will? It was because the time did not align with Jesus. In other words, he did not have the environmental conditions to fulfill it. 

The time had not matured for all the people, from top to bottom, left to right, to be united in fully welcoming Jesus. Therefore, Jesus spent three years adjusting the timing. 

However, because Jesus' three years of preparation to align the timing went awry, he left behind the time that we must fulfill through 2,000 years of history. This is how it happened. 

So what about our Unification Church today? The Unification Church has also failed to align with that timing. When the Unification Church started in the Republic of Korea, it did not stand on a common ground where the church could respond to God's Will. Due to this backlash and conflict, we missed many opportunities for timing. We missed countless opportunities and entered the 1970s. 

So, in the process of time flowing by, when can we see the end of the Will and the fulfillment of the Will? That time must certainly be present in our Unification Church course. Of course, the 1960s were also a time to fulfill the Will.
The 1970s will remain a significant era. However, if we consider which period is more precious, the 1970s are more important than the 1960s.  
The 1960s were a foundational era, while the 1970s are a practical era.  
From a meaningful perspective, up until the 1960s, it was a period to lay the groundwork for the church. It was a time to establish the foundation of the church. What this means is that, although Christianity had opposed it until now, it was a period to overcome that opposition and prepare an external environment that would not resist it.  
Originally, Christianity should have borne fruit centered on a 6,000-year history. However, due to the opposition from Christianity, our Unification Church itself has paved a path to meet the right time. We must recognize that this era is the 1960s. In other words, this era was a time of indemnity for us.  
Christianity, which was to bear fruit during the historical indemnity period of 6,000 years and achieve the ideal purpose, could not fulfill that purpose, so there had to be a period of horizontal re-indemnity. That period was the 1960s. During this time, we had to pay the price with tears, with blood, or with all other sacrifices.  
Although we paid such a price, it was not a price that could confidently be rewarded by God. Nor was it a price that would disappear forever. When a thousand people pay the price, it brings about the fruits that a thousand people can receive, but the price we paid in the 1960s only became a condition for the Unification Church to meet the right time; it did not bring about results that could fulfill that time.  
So what about the 1970s? It is a time when, if we make sacrifices, we can receive rewards proportional to those sacrifices. In that sense, the 1960s and 1970s are different eras. What this means is that there is a time to lay the foundation for any work, a time to practice, and then a time to achieve. However, without a foundation being laid, one cannot practice, and without practice, one cannot achieve.  
Thus, for our Unification Church, the 1960s were a time to lay the groundwork. In other words, it was a time to come out under the banner of religion and lay the foundation as the Unification Church.  
Now, the 1970s are a time for practical implementation in the Unification Church. Achievement cannot occur without going through a process of practice. Even if the foundation has been laid, achievement cannot happen with just the foundation. The practical time of how to implement this or how to practice it is more important.  
There is a time in spring when farmers sow seeds, a time when the sown seeds sprout and grow, and a time for harvesting. Similarly, there is a time for laying the groundwork to sow seeds and a time for growth, that is, a time for practice. This practical time is the most crucial time that determines everything. Therefore, we must do well in this time. For our Unification Church, the 1970s are a time for practice.  
What should we practice for? It is a time to practice for the fulfillment of the purpose.  
Then, will everything we practice disappear along with history? No, it will not disappear; rather, it will bring about the fruits necessary for fulfilling the purpose.  
When seeds are sown and they grow, the seeds disappear. However, from the price paid for the seeds that have disappeared, a new life sprouts. The seed and the life are absolutely different. Therefore, if it is rice, the rice must undergo the owner's various efforts until it bears fruit centered on this life. Fertilizer must be given, and all the benefits of heaven and earth must be applied for it to bear fruit.  
Because of all the efforts we made in the 1960s, a single sprout called the Unification Church has emerged. Today, there are countless religions on this earth. In terms of grains, it is like many grains being sown in fields or meadows. Just as rice, barley, or corn are sown, the Unification Church has finally sprouted and started to show its existence with a green hue.  
Become those who influence the world.  
So what is the issue from now on? It is how to mature this and bear the perfect fruit that God desires. When we look at the laws of nature, we are in an important time. In other words, we have arrived at the most precious time as a practical time to fulfill the purpose.  
Since we are entering the practical era this year on the foundation laid in the past, it is even more precious.  
By 1974, the second seven-year course will end. From 1975 to 1981 is the period of the third seven-year course. Thus, the 1970s are the most crucial time for our Unification Church, connecting the second and third seven-year courses to the final turning point.  
The time has already matured, and the environment to welcome the practical era we have longed for has arrived. In this practical era, what position do those who can practice hold? The time has come with the environmental conditions to fulfill the purpose, so what about ourselves, who must practice centered on this time? This cannot be a trivial matter.  
Now, when we look at Christianity or the world’s overall situation, those who oppose us are not stepping on us; rather, they have entered a realm where they can be influenced by our movements. If we compare this to a day, they are in the sunset, while we are welcoming the morning. The sunlight of the sunset will gradually darken into night as time goes on, while the sunlight of the morning will become bright daylight as time goes on. Therefore, we have truly reached a critical time for the practical process.  
Now, if you understand that the time is ripe, you must do everything as humans to influence the world. If you fail to influence, you will be slandered. That is how it will be.  
The Israelite people could not match the time centered on Jesus, and as a result, they wandered for 2,000 years to revive that time. They did so even during the time of laying the foundation, but today, if we are in a process where we can achieve, and we are in an environment to practice while looking forward to the fulfillment of the purpose, what will happen if we cannot match this time? If the Israelite people could not match the time during the era of laying the foundation and had to endure 2,000 years of suffering to find a time for revival, will the fate that will befall our Unification Church or the Republic of Korea not be more miserable?  
Considering that we are in such a position, the members of our Unification Church must unite and utilize this time, which is a good time for practice, in every possible way. This is the responsibility that the Unification believers must take in the coming 1970s, isn’t it? You must keep this issue in mind.  
Three Absolute Factors for Indemnity and Restoration Completion  
So, when the time and the people are ready to achieve, what is necessary? Conditions are absolutely necessary. No matter how capable a person is, or how well the time is prepared, the conditions must be presented. The conditions to be presented differ for each of you. Since each person has different innate qualities and dispositions, the path of indemnity each must take is also different. Indemnity and restoration completion require people, time, and conditions. These are absolute factors. Therefore, although our individual dispositions differ, we now have character and have met the time, so conditions are needed here. What will these conditions be? There must be a proper direction.  
Your nature and the direction you must go must align with the standards that God sees. "Father, not my will, but Yours be done." Until that moment, the directions do not align. My will does not align with the Father’s will.  
Thus, the direction must be aligned. Conditions must be presented from a position where the direction is aligned. For example, if God is looking east, and you present conditions while looking west, it will not work. You must present conditions from a position aligned with God.  
So what are those conditions? They are the conditions lost by Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden. They lost the word, the reality, and the heart. In other words, the three great offerings are for the purpose of recovering these. So what are the three great offerings? Ultimately, it is about finding sons and daughters. The three great offerings are that.  
During the 40-day period, what is to be done centered on that 40-day period? In that 40-day period, the three great conditions are to find three great sons and daughters. That is, it is about finding three people. These three people correspond to the three sons of the Old Testament, New Testament, and Completed Testament eras. Additionally, these conditions correspond to the three angels and can also represent the three generations. For example, they can represent Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob. They can also refer to my father, myself, and my descendants.  
From a horizontal perspective, when viewed from my center, they also become the representative forms of the son-in-law generation. To restore all these conditions, how must it be done? It must be in unity with the word. You must become a person who is one with the word. However, even if one is united with the word, if the heart does not align with God, it cannot be done.  
Therefore, in establishing the direction, it must be aligned with the word that God aims for, the direction that aligns with God’s character, and the direction that aligns with God’s heart. Here, we can restore the sons and daughters of faith who become the conditions for indemnity.  
When Jesus took three disciples to the Garden of Gethsemane to pray, there was a misalignment of direction between Jesus and the three disciples. Although it seemed that the conditions and forms of the three sons were fulfilled, the will of Jesus and the will of the disciples were different. There was a difference between God’s will and Jesus’ will, and also a difference between Jesus’ will and the disciples’ will. God’s will must have been Jesus’ will, and Jesus’ will must have been the disciples’ will.  
Centered on Jesus, who represents God above and the earth below, they should have moved toward a unified goal that aligns with the three stages of rebirth, growth, and completion. However, they struggled from conflicting positions, which was the prayer in the Garden of Gethsemane. The content of praying three times reflects this. Why did He pray three times when one prayer would have sufficed? There is a problem here.  
From this perspective, the will of the Father, your will, and the will of the sons and daughters of faith you will restore must align. These three wills must become one vertically, and centered on this, God, you, and your faith’s sons and daughters must become one. Since the vertical must be indemnified horizontally, it must necessarily be three sons. In that position, conditions must be presented.  
Therefore, unless the time is aligned, the people are aligned, and the direction is aligned, conditions cannot be presented, and the purpose cannot be fulfilled. No matter how much you pray, "Oh purpose, let it be fulfilled," if you are not in a position of alignment, that grace cannot become yours. Grace must meet the time and pass through that moment. It is not enough to merely have the time itself. Only when the will that God desires and my will are aligned, and when the conditions that God desires and the conditions I present are aligned, can the purpose be fulfilled.  
The three generations must unite to form the son-in-law generation.  
From the perspective of the 1970s, the teacher feels a sense of responsibility. I know that there is a responsibility. As we enter the 1970s, we have already reached a position where we can welcome the time that God has prepared. Therefore, we must present the conditions that can be aligned with this.  
The conditions to be presented include those that the teacher himself must offer, as well as those that the Unification Church must offer.  
In other words, just as God’s will, Jesus’ will, and the disciples’ will must align, God’s will, the will centered on the Unification Church, and the teacher’s will must also align. Additionally, your will toward the teacher must align with the teacher’s will.  
For alignment to occur, it must be a straight line. Alignment cannot occur when each is in a separate position. You cannot try to align based on yourself. You must align in a straight line with each other.  
That is why Jesus had to align God’s will with his own will. Then, he had to align with the will of the disciples. However, that did not happen. If that happens, even if one tries to go their own way, they cannot. They cannot take any path beyond the cross. They cannot make such a decision.  
To fulfill the purpose, one must already have decided the path and stand on a decisive foundation. In other words, one must align with God’s will centered on a single purpose and direction. Everything must be in unity; otherwise, it cannot be done.  
Among those who have fallen away from believing in the Unification Church, there are some who say, "The teachings of the Unification Church are good, but do I really have to go to church? I can live according to those teachings without going to church." That is not how it works. You must come to church because you need to indemnify the vertical history horizontally. It is clearly stated in the principle.  
Then, when we look at the Unification Church itself, God’s will, the teacher’s will, and your will must align. That must be the first step. After that, you must set the direction, and then you must present the conditions. Without that alignment, no matter how ripe the time is, the fulfillment of the purpose is absolutely impossible. These three must come together and stand in a position similar to that of a single offering. When viewed from the perspective of the entire universe, there is only one path to unity.  
Therefore, what has God labored for until now? He has raised people who align with His will and made their descendants align with them. Achieving this alignment is the son-in-law generation. When we look at families, it is three generations. Centered on God, Adam and his children ultimately form three generations. Is that not so? Why is the son-in-law generation necessary? Because when this is achieved, the purpose will be fulfilled. However, if the son-in-law generation is not completed, a world where the vertical and horizontal alignments are achieved will not come to pass. The son-in-law generation refers to the alignment of three generations.  
In the time of Jesus, the people who were to form the son-in-law generation centered on God were Peter, James, and John. However, they could not unite. If they do not unite, the purpose cannot be fulfilled. As a result, God's suffering remained as God's suffering, Jesus' suffering remained as Jesus' suffering, and the disciples' suffering remained as the disciples' suffering.  
That suffering also became divided and did not achieve unity. They did not suffer from a unified heart. God felt His own distress, Jesus felt His own distress, and the disciples felt their own distress.  
So when does the suffering of these three generations become united? It does not cross the peak of death.
Because it cannot be bound, Peter, James, and John were able to stand in a place that transcended the valley of death through Jesus. Consequently, they were finally able to align with the will of Jesus and the will of God. Without this, alignment would not have been possible.  
The disciples, who caused distress to God and Jesus, would have had no way to be redeemed forever, but by crossing over the path of death, they established a foundation of heart and a foundation of practice. As a result, they positioned themselves in alignment with the will, which had previously been contrary to their own. This is how it is viewed.  
The issue is yourselves.  
God's will is not vague. So how is God's will specifically defined? Today, God has a clear will regarding this nation. You must become individuals who can take responsibility for this will of God. After becoming such individuals, you must become such families, and then such clans, nations, and states. You must become people who can take responsibility for this. That is why people are important.

This unity of heart is absolutely necessary in our lives, from daily living to the course of a year, and even throughout our entire lives, as well as in the entire historical process.

Even in our daily lives, if we leave home in the morning with one heart but return in the evening with two hearts, we cannot achieve a single purpose. When we look at it this way, we realize that the society we live in today, and the living environment you are currently facing, does not have a unified heart. If it is difficult to achieve a purpose with one heart, it is even more impossible to fulfill a single purpose with two hearts.

When we look at everything in this way, we see that a united heart is necessary. Anyone can start with one heart, forge ahead with one heart, and pursue the results of that unity for a longer period; the greater the duration, the greater the desired purpose will be.

We must have one heart. In pursuing any purpose, we must have one heart. Without a united heart, it is impossible to achieve that purpose. When we observe this, we can see that when God created the heavens and the earth, He did not do so with a divided heart. Since history must aim for one purpose, it is inevitable that numerous ideologies and thoughts will converge into a world that seeks that one purpose.

The convergence into such a world of purpose cannot happen by chance. Therefore, behind the pursuit of one world, an absolute factor and a point of agreement must be fulfilled; otherwise, one world cannot be established. In other words, through the unified origin, we go through a process, and through that process, we can achieve a world.

To be happy, what worldview does the current global ideology reflect? It is divided into a materialistic worldview and a spiritual worldview. In other words, materialism and idealism are in opposition. Can we move toward a center from this opposing stance of material and spiritual? That is impossible. When we look at humanity, we see that we are made of body and mind. The mind cannot analyze or process the realities we face.

Although it seems that the world of the mind does not have concrete content, it governs the material world. Therefore, at this point in South Korea, centered on the 1970s, we must not emphasize only the material aspect, that is, economic revival. If humanity continues to exist in a divided state, it cannot avoid misery. Without a point of agreement, one cannot achieve a single purpose. If one cannot achieve a single purpose, there can be no happiness or peace for that person, that nation, or that world. Happiness cannot exist while leaving conflicting factors between the two.

When we look at a family, if the husband and wife hold opposing positions, there can be no peace in that family. The subject must be the center. The object must revolve around the subject and connect itself to the subject. Only then can the object achieve its purpose. However, if the subject stands in the position of the object, it cannot achieve a single purpose. When we see this, we understand that to achieve a purpose in a family, the internal and external aspects of that family must unite.
