Establishment of Truth
When we look at a person, we often say that their family seems to be a good family. This is because they were born in a position where they can guarantee their past. That story...
You can evaluate a household by looking at its members, assess a person by observing their present state, and glimpse into the future by observing that person. From this perspective, oneself is an extension of the past, a condensation of the present, and a starting point for the future. 

From this point of view, happiness becomes the center of victory in the past, the center of victory in the present, and a new starting point for the future. In other words, to be happy, the past, present, and future must all be unified. This is the meaning of pursuing what is true. 

The sages who have appeared throughout history are more genuine than anyone who has come and gone in the historical process. So, where does truth come from? Truth is not established only in the future or only in the present. Truth must also be true in the past, true in the present, and can be true in the future. Truth transcends the environment. A true person is the center in the past, the center in the present, and also the center in the future. It is from this position that a true person is established. 

Then, what can come closest to truth in the human world? Many people have come and gone, but what is closest to truth is not a relative teacher or parent, but oneself. So, what is the closest relative of truth to oneself? It is one’s own heart, that is, one’s conscience. We often say that a person is conscientious or that their heart is upright. What does it mean for the heart to be upright? History proceeds directly. Therefore, the past must be upright, the present must be upright, and the future must also be upright. 

If the past is bent, then the present can be bent, and the future can also be bent. We must innovate such connections and go to a place where the heart can proceed directly. Directness is a line that connects two points. What are those two points? Cause and effect. What is the cause made of? It is made of one heart. Then what is the result? It must be one heart. In other words, the phenomenon of drawing one purpose through one heart foundation is a straight line. 

Therefore, happiness is established from the position of truth, and God's providence progresses from the position of truth. So, this truth is the issue. Within this truth, a true self is needed. Because one has not become that true self, they are going through education and cultivation. Thus, today’s educational system is structured around the issue of human transformation, and that has been the focus of the innovation movement so far. However, the position of truth has not yet been determined. 

What can determine that truth? It is something that is contrary to the superficial purposes demanded by humanity. It is not superficial. It is absolute and central content. What is it? Is it money? No. 

Happiness cannot be discussed solely in economic terms. No matter how much of a hero one may be who unites the world in their palm, if they are to sing of happiness, the joy that overflows in their heart while looking at the global stage they have established must become the ideal of the world. Without that, one cannot sing of happiness. That joy must not be just one’s own joy; it must be the position where the closest people can also appreciate the fulfillment of that purpose as their ideal, and only then does happiness unfold. 

Looking at the historical process so far, history has been a history of struggle. When looking at a country, when a ruler, along with their ministers, successfully establishes national policy centered around their ministers and reaches a position of fulfillment, can the whole nation rejoice based on the fulfillment of that policy? Can they praise and rejoice in the success of that policy? The phenomena that appear are diverse. 

When looking at so-called democratic countries with a two-party system today, whenever the ruling party proposes something, the opposition party unconditionally opposes it. Such a situation cannot be a requirement for happiness. The requirements for happiness must not be pursued from an external standpoint. When the relative environment is established all around, where a person can think of their achieved happiness as the happiness of their ideal, then that happiness can be eternally guaranteed. 

The reason parental love is needed
What establishes such a position? It is not established by external factors. It is not created by social systems. It is established by heart, that is, love. That love does not appear suddenly. It comes from the past. That love connects to the present and extends to the future. 

Then, who is the absolute center of that love? It is not a person. A person cannot be the absolute center. Because people seek absolute goodness, they cannot help but pursue love that can be placed at the absolute center. We call this God's love. 

Even in the world, no matter how unworthy a child may be, parents love that child. Parental love transcends good and bad external conditions. No matter how flawed the parents may be, their love for their child is absolute. That is why parental love is necessary. 

So why is parental love necessary? It is because parents can serve as the foundation of love that can replace past connections. Only by standing on that foundation can one become a child of love and enter a position where they can be grafted into love. That is why it is said that a person who does not have parents is unfortunate. In other words, through parental love, we can inherit the connections and victories of the past from our parents. To say that one has received parental love means that they can hold onto the past as it is. 

Therefore, if there is a child who has received parental love, they will share their fate with their parents until they grow old and die. When there is an inheritance from parents, that inheritance does not last until one grows old and dies. Such external things will eventually fade away and disappear, but the love connected to parents is eternal. The more miserable the external situation, the deeper one can delve into it, become more united, and have even greater connections. What is that? It is love. 

What can determine the victory of the past? It is neither the authority of the world nor material possessions. It is undoubtedly parental love. Therefore, a person who has received parental love can bloom in reality without knowing why. They can flourish in reality. It becomes a natural and blessed touch. On the other hand, a person who has grown up with some unknown internal flaws, that is, emotional flaws, and has grown up in a repressive environment cannot become a loyal and respected person from all sides. 

Then, when looking at the overall global situation today, where is the source of the flaws that have appeared worldwide? It is not solely because of flaws in the social organization that has established today's cultural world, nor is it solely because of flaws in the people who operate it. So, what is it due to? It is due to emotional flaws. Emotional flaws create defects in society through their influence. This is acknowledged by all. 

From this perspective, when we look at ourselves, the issue becomes how to become children who can align with the love that parents had for us. This issue becomes the absolute factor that can determine the happiness or unhappiness of a family. Even if a couple lives happily, if their child does not align with the parents' heart, unhappiness is bound to arise. When there are sons and daughters, happiness cannot be achieved if only the son aligns with the parents' heart. The daughter must also align. This is how it is.

The original mission entrusted to humanity  
For everything on this earth to exist, there must be a cause for its existence. The society we live in today, the country we are in, and the world we see are all in the position of results. For all these environmental connections to be established, there must be a motivation for that environment to be established, which we cannot deny.  
Furthermore, when we look at the formation of a society, a nation, and a world, it is, of course, us humans who carry that forward. However, the fundamental cause for the formation of humans cannot be humans themselves. Therefore, humans cannot escape the position of being a resultant existence. Because of this, there must be a motivation and content that allows humans to be formed, and there must be a cause.  
Among us humans, there are infinite hopes, infinite desires, and infinite ideals. For us, who are the reality of results, to become such beings, there must first be a reality of cause that can allow that. That reality of cause is what we call God.  
Because God is a personal deity, He is the overall motivation and cause for us humans. Because the cause, God, possesses such content, the resultant humans cannot help but possess similar content. Therefore, the God who is the cause and we humans who are the result must manifest as an inseparable conclusion centered on the human world. This is God's desire to find humanity.  
Just as a farmer plows the field and sows seeds in spring to reap many fruits through those seeds, God's purpose in creating humanity was not limited to Adam and Eve but was to reap the world through Adam and Eve.  
When we consider this fact, we can see that the world is originally a comprehensive symbol that can realize God's ideals. This comprehensive symbol has the mission to complete the ideal garden of God's infinite love centered on the entire world. This mission is connected to the dual worlds that must be completed, not only on earth but also in the spiritual world.  
In light of this, the mission that our individual beings possess is not to live for seventy, eighty years, or less than a century to achieve our own individual desires, but to live to complete and fulfill the entire ideological world of the cosmos. We must recognize that this is the purpose of our birth and our lives.  
When we realize that this tremendous creation of God was to give life to the ancestors of humanity, we will understand how much God has longed for the day when humanity would possess life and achieve globalization in the process of that life.  
However, contrary to such divine desires, we must recognize that the fact that we have seen the beginning of sorrowful grief is an unbearable sorrow for God, who is connected to this universe and all of humanity.  
This sorrow and grief are greater than any sorrow and grief in history. Therefore, unless we welcome the day when this sorrow and grief are removed from this earth, we cannot pursue the factors of happiness in our lives. No matter how great the dreams an individual holds, it is inevitable that those dreams cannot be realized.  
The mission of the Unification Church  
So, what is the purpose for which we humans dedicate our lives today? It is not the realization of the ideal world. More importantly, it remains as our life’s purpose to resolve the sorrow and grief that are bound to God, who is the primary motivation. We must reflect once again on the saying that life is a vale of tears because we are in this life journey.  
The sorrowful life is because it has become a connection to the sorrowful God, which we cannot deny. When we understand this, we must ask ourselves, where do we go? We were born as descendants of the fall, unable to go toward the world of happiness. Therefore, we must seek a way to resolve the basis of resentment caused by the fall, and even if it means dying, we must struggle and search until we resolve this. We cannot deny that we are on a fateful path.  
Then, looking at the historical fact that we were born in such a position, lived in such a position, and died in such a position, has there been anyone who has stepped forward to take responsibility for solving these problems on this earth? Has there been a saint who has stepped forward to take responsibility for breaking down the basis of this resentment? Has there been a savior who has taken on such responsibility? Considering this historical reality, what is the mission that our Unification Church must undertake today? It is not the realization of the ideal world, but we must recognize that our primary mission remains to demolish the basis of this resentment.  
As we look back over the past 50 years, the days we repented were not the days of joy that God desired, but if there are stories that have been intertwined in the historical flow, we hope that they will become days of settlement that can demolish the basis of resentment left in the historical process. However, even now, we do not have a free place to welcome the days of joy.

Therefore, the multitude of unification must become pioneers of God who can break through this darkness and fill the pit of resentment, the more they look at these facts. The boundary we must cross in the 1970s

The mission entrusted to us in the Republic of Korea
The people have opposed the Unification Church until today. However, the Unification Church was not established because it wanted to create a sect. When we meet again, if we leave conditions such as revenge or indemnity, there would be resentment left in heaven, so I understood that I had to be in a position to pray for the enemy while looking back.

Having avoided this path of being chased, this path of being driven away, this path of exile, I have now reached the shoreline. And I have stood at the very edge of the shoreline. God has established a new appearance of a son there, giving new equipment, and has come this far with the destiny of national confrontation. Every time the teacher broke through the enemy's ranks, he thought of God's heart. I understood that without having the heart of a servant, one could not lay such a foundation. When we went out to evangelize in the regions, we were ridiculed by people of all ages. There were times when a police officer grabbed one of our members by the collar. We were treated like stepchildren and sinners, and I know there have been times when we were beaten in unjust situations. When I think of this, how much more sorrowful must God be than we are? How much more pitiful must God feel than we do?

If a king of a country fled as his nation fell and collapsed before the enemy's sword, how pitiful must the prince born as the king's son be before the enemy? We have walked this path with such a form.

We must also thank the Father for not allowing us to face a second death. How much effort has God made to keep us alive? We, who were foolish, struggled in the regions. When our young boys and girls went out to work, there were those who opposed us, but on the other hand, there were those who came to see us even at night. Even when parents opposed us, those second-generation children worried about our hunger and brought us food wrapped in handkerchiefs. We have gone through such history. This is not because we are even a little better. It is because God, who sees this, feels pity and has the responsibility to protect us.

When the Father, who holds all authority in heaven, sacrifices for us in such a miserable position, we must understand how much His dignity has fallen to the ground. We often recall and long for those times. However, while we boast of the compassionate hearts we felt then and the connections of the environment that were established at that time, we have forgotten the circumstances of the Father, who was miserable behind that environment.

But you must never forget this. Do you reminisce about the good days of the past, or the 1960s, when you shed tears of blood and prayed all night with the teacher? Of course, those are days to remember. However, we must understand how miserable and unjust God was behind those days. I sincerely hope you can have the attitude to commemorate that day and reflect on it.

Blessing and National Restoration
This year, we plan to do something that will become widely known around the world. Does anyone among you know what that is? "It's the blessing." Yes, it is the blessing. Just think about it: about 700 couples will have a joint wedding ceremony. That is by no means an easy task.

The mindset that the blessed individuals must adopt
Many young men and women are here, and they may be curious about the blessing. As they gathered here, they might have wondered when young men and women would gather like this again. Surely that was the case.

Starting in March, we plan to gather young men and women from all over the country for special training. However, if we are to pair 700 couples, even if we decide five pairs a day, it will take about 140 days. That means it will take about five months. Right? During those five months, they will think only about the blessing, whether they are sleeping or eating. They will wrestle with the issue of the blessing for about five months.

In that case, while the young men and women will be happy to be blessed, it will be a huge problem for the teacher, who has to take full responsibility for everything. 

For the teacher, it feels like being dragged in to be tortured by the Japanese during the colonial period. When I think about how to get through this, it feels like having to crawl through a long tunnel filled with poison gas.

Therefore, what I ask of those who will attend the upcoming special training is that they do not cause any trouble at that time. Today, as you celebrate the teacher's birthday, I ask you to understand this situation of the teacher.

According to precedent,
Before deciding on the partner to be blessed, the Father will surely choose someone who is the right person, so we must absolutely obey and submit. However, when it comes to deciding on their own husband or wife, no matter how unattractive the person is, when they see the photo of the other person, they ask, "What about this person?" and no one looks at it with a happy expression. I have never seen anyone look at it with wide-open eyes and say, "Let's see." Everyone frowns when they look at it. On such days, the teacher feels bad all day long.

I hope that the young men and women here will show a happier expression when they face the photos of the person who will be their husband or wife when they are called to be evaluated by the teacher. Everyone comes and glances at the photo presented by the teacher, and if the person looks better than they expected, they are happy, and if they look worse than they expected, their facial expression sours. (Laughter)

The ideal partner
If you ask many people to choose their partner freely, they cannot choose their ideal partner. If there is an east, there is a west; if there is a south, there is a north. Therefore, if an east-type person meets another east-type person, it cannot be an ideal meeting because there is no west. Likewise, if a south-type person meets another south-type person, it cannot be ideal because there is no north. Therefore, east-type people must seek out west-type people, and south-type people must seek out north-type people. Do you understand what I mean?

Let’s say there is a person whose face is long like a horse. What is a face that is longer than that horse face? It is a grasshopper face, right? (Laughter) If that person is paired with a grasshopper-faced person, what kind of children will they have? Think about what kind of children they will have. Surely, they will have children that look like lizards. (Laughter) That’s how it is. It is the principle of nature. Therefore, everyone is paired with the opposite type. A person who looks like a horse should be paired with someone who is broad like a pumpkin or a gourd. Only then can the opposite types harmonize well, and if they produce offspring, at least one or two of them will be useful children. However, if they do not do this and just pair with someone they like, then all the offspring will be useless.

Therefore, when the teacher pairs people, what should they believe in when they marry? They should marry not based on who looks good to their eyes but to produce good sons and daughters in the future. They should marry for the sake of their children. If you pair with someone you like and have children, but those children are such that no man or woman in the world would want to look at them, what would happen? There is no greater misfortune than that. They will be unhappy for their entire lives. It is worse than being unhappy because of one's own flaws or shortcomings.

Thus, our marriages are for the sake of our descendants. So, while the appearances of the marrying parties may differ, the problem is how to match them with people who can give birth to children who resemble only their good traits.

The blessing is for the descendants
The teacher has married many people up until now. The teacher will have records of marrying people worldwide. If this time 700 couples are married, it may remain as an eternal record. Isn’t that so?

Recently, the teacher finished a tour of Jeonnam. There was a woman I remembered from when she was blessed, but I don't know if her husband is here. I wonder if that woman came along too. We will only do it for about three days. At most, about 10,000 people can fit in the Jangchung Gymnasium, and if we hold the ceremony there, how many people will gather? If there is a wedding at 2 PM, people will probably start lining up from early morning. Tens of thousands will come. At that time, the teacher will become the narrator, grab the microphone, make everyone laugh, and say, "Let's gather our gifts here." It may seem rude to receive gifts, but we can set the rules ourselves. In a democratic system, the majority decides, and the minority must comply. This is the principle of democracy.

So, the people gathered here are those who have come to present a way for this nation to survive with innovative content for a new era, and how glorious it would be if they give gifts on this blessed day. After making the announcement, we will say, "Those who want to give gifts, raise your hands." Then, they will end up giving gifts. In this way, we can also receive gifts.

Then, we will close the doors and sell admission tickets for 10,000 won each. If we say we are selling admission tickets for 10,000 won, we can't just let people in. 10,000 won is a bargain. If you want to enter, it doesn't matter if you have no money, but if you have money, is 10,000 won a problem? Will you pay 10,000 won to enter or not? "I will." Women may not know, but all men, ten out of ten, one hundred percent will enter. Isn't that right? "Yes."

If only 10,000 people enter, at 10,000 won each, that would be 1 billion won. With 1 billion, we can pay off all the costs and interest and still have some left over. All the expenses will come from there. Wow, that's just great! (Laughter) However, since those people set the condition that they contributed through admission tickets, we can't just let them go.

Now, everyone, in 1970, there were 700 people. So, shouldn't we give them something too? Then is it 7 won, 70 won, or 700 won? Is it 70,000 won, 700,000 won, 7 million won, 70 million won, or 700 million won? Now, let's hear your answers. This man, how much should it be? "It should be 700 won." Just 700 won? I would rather set it at 70 won. (Laughter) Even an elementary school student would say that for such a celebration, it should be more than 700 won. So, officially, everyone from children to adults should give at least 700 won. 70 won is too little, and 7 won is not even worth mentioning. Therefore, you might think that it should be more than 7,000 won, but I am being lenient. Should we set it at 70 won? 70 won is not even enough for a bowl of noodles. At the very least, you should treat your parents to lunch, right? Since it is a blessing, if you are preparing for a celebration, shouldn't you treat them to a meal of bulgogi? Even if you skip that, the automatic decision based on the majority opinion should conclude that it should be more than 700 won. Isn't that right? "Yes." So, 70 years, 700 pairs, 700 won, that's how it goes. So, if you have money, will you pay or not? "I will." Those who say they will pay, raise your hands. There are some who didn't raise their hands, but I believe you will cooperate. (Laughter) Here, men, will you pay or not? "I will." Let's decide among ourselves and move on. This is not compulsory.

In this situation, how can you not give gifts and say you will help elsewhere? That won't work. Therefore, for this event, all our Unification Church members across the country must contribute 700 won. Has that been decided? "Yes." Now, the district leaders are here, the regional leaders are here, the youth are here, and all the key personnel who can spread this message to various regions are here, so the content decided by the teacher will be communicated to all Unification Church members across the country within a week.

The gifts should come from grandmothers, grandfathers, and children aged 18 and above. Then, about 10 million won will come out.

Did you earn a lot? By promoting for over an hour, we have earned 10 million won. (Laughter) Do you feel good or bad? "Good." Just from what you heard today, you will feel good.

So, will it only be for Korea? No. Given our situation, if the chairman of the Japan branch comes and asks how much should we contribute, if Japan contributes 7,000 won each, how much will that be? Do you understand? When I asked the head of the Japan business department if Korea could raise 10 million won, would Japan contribute 20 million won? He said okay and left. That was also commanded by the teacher. Even if we earn money, we can't spend it without the teacher's approval.

In the end, even if I tell the Unification Church members around the world not to participate, they will participate. Why? Because if Japan participates, why can't we? That's what they will say. If the teacher goes to that country and promotes, everyone will be excited. However, since I can't go right now, I am promoting here.

So, in this way, people from all over the world will join in.
is not going to be easy. 

This is about sending a bride and groom from their country for the sake of their dignity. In this case, several tens of millions of won will not be a problem. Do you understand? If we can gather about 30 million won, the teacher might contribute 30 million won as well. Although there is no money, if it is necessary, it will be done. The teacher hopes it would be around 100 million won.

Prayer to mobilize the world
So what should the bride and groom do? They should invite their parents, relatives, and even distant relatives to come if they want. However, since the admission ticket is 700 won each, everyone must buy an admission ticket. And those who cannot sell 10 tickets will not be allowed to attend the wedding. So, will they sell them or not? (laughter) 

Then what will we do with the money collected? We will create a 3.7 scholarship foundation and use it for scholarships. Why? Because there are too many children being born like beggars. This is frightening. We thought they would only have a few, but they keep having them. (laughter) 

If about 15,000 people come to the Jangchung Gymnasium, we can expect about 10 million won. Then, if we add the 10 million won from our church itself and the money coming from other countries, it will be at least 50 million won. 

If 15,000 people gather and pay 700 won each to enter, when will there be time to calculate change? They will be pushing in with two 500 won bills. When will they be able to receive change? It will definitely happen that way. Also, if there are any business owners among the relatives, we should conduct a special donation campaign for the young people who will take responsibility for the prosperity of humanity and South Korea. If we announce that a certain business owner contributed a certain amount for the wedding of 700 couples and highlight a few famous people, others will feel compelled to contribute for the sake of their reputation. (laughter) Are you smiling because you feel good or because you feel bad? "I am smiling because I feel good."

This time, we must do it this way. This is for the sake of your children in the future. Centered around the wedding ceremony of 700 couples, think back to the year 1977, which will be seven years from now. Therefore, from now on, if the teacher encourages you to put in your utmost effort and fulfill your responsibilities to overcome the seven-year hurdle, you will do so.

Then, as time goes on, this money will grow into a massive fund. This will enable us to buy up all the companies in the world in the future. If we deposit all this money in one bank and withdraw it all at once, that bank will have no choice but to come to us. (laughter) This is not a joke. The teacher is conducting such research.

Will there be problems in Korea if this happens? "Yes." As soon as such problems arise in Korea, reporters from media outlets around the world will come and broadcast live globally. When we held the blessing ceremony for 430 couples before, the Dutch members were dancing with the television on, and it broke down when it was time to finish. Such things will happen again this time.

Then mobilizing several tens of millions of people will not be a problem. How many will be mobilized globally? Every person will see it. You need to understand that this can become a driving force that brings about a thousand fortunes in the future. Therefore, what should you do? You must pray. Do you understand? "Yes." Then you should contribute. "Yes."

Infinite tourism resources
What time is it now? "It’s 6 o'clock." It has been exactly six hours. It took six hours to hold this feast.

You may not know how our Unification Church is moving right now. You have all worked hard until now. Even while being chased around, you have initiated various movements, and now we are doing it splendidly.

Now we have taken on the history of Korea centered around Japan. Right now, our organization is connected from Hokkaido to Kyushu. The Japanese members have the spirit to do anything as long as they are commanded, so we are planning to use our organization across Japan to bring high school students on graduation trips to Korea. If that doesn’t work, we are preparing to do so through the Japanese Minister of Education. We want all high school students in Japan to come to Korea for school trips.

To do this, we are currently holding a Japan-Korea hunting competition. We are planning to call the leaders and make them all spearheads. If this plan is realized, we will set up an office in Korea and arrange several courses with groups of 200 people at a time. When they come to Korea, they will all bring dollars with them. Isn’t that right? It’s not just by exporting goods that we earn dollars. Even if we bring in just 200 people at a time through such operations, a vast amount of funds will come in. Isn’t that right?

If we create routes in all directions, such as an eastern course and a western course, we can bring in several thousand people at once. We are planning to create a tourism company this way. Then what will we do with them? Since they are high school students, the Victory Alliance will be behind them to provide education. We plan to conduct tours through the Sale Tourism Company. Sale Tourism means the world’s best tourism company and also a tourism company aimed at unifying the world. We will create a Sale Tourism Company in that sense.

Then how will we handle these young students from Japan? We need to educate them anew. Japan is currently in danger of being swept into communism. How will we save Japan, which is in such a situation? We will bring high school students to educate them.

When they come to Korea, we will introduce Korean culture. We will take them around for tours. We also plan to build a large theater in Seoul that can accommodate about a thousand people and take them there to introduce Korean culture.

We will explain what kind of country Korea is and what its culture is like. We will also introduce the fact that all Japanese culture, including Buddhism, was transmitted through Korea, ultimately showing that Korea is the ancestral nation of Japanese culture. Then we will introduce Korean customs and explain the urgent situation of Korea, which is currently surrounded by the communist world, while emphasizing that the most important issue for Korea moving forward is the anti-communism issue and that the Victory Alliance has been organized for this purpose.

Thus, we will either have them take home a commemorative item from their visit to Korea or leave something they can boast about. So what will they leave behind? As a friendly delegation, they will stimulate this country as high school students. The most needed stimulation for this country is the anti-communist movement, so they will provide that stimulation. We will create anti-communist leaflets and have them distribute them all around Korea. They will go around various regions distributing anti-communist leaflets.

What will happen when they distribute anti-communist leaflets in Korea and return to Japan? They will promote that high school students went to Korea, distributed anti-communist leaflets, and engaged in the anti-communist movement. However, among the parents of those students, there may be communists. Then those parents will scold their children, saying, "Oh, you little rascal, I send you to school, and you go to Korea to distribute anti-communist leaflets!" The children will respond, "But I feel good, why are you acting like this, Mom and Dad?" This is the kind of issue that will arise. This is how we will educate to save Japan from the communist world.

So we need to create a way to survive, right? "Yes." If North Korea invades the South and the situation becomes urgent, where will we go? Where will we enter from Busan? We will enter the Pacific Ocean. At that time, we will call the president of the Japan Shipping Promotion Association and ask him to bring several thousand-ton ships. It will happen. At that time, only the Unification Church members will… (laughter) If you don’t think about that, you are foolish. That’s why the teacher is preparing everything. There’s no need to talk about this.

By doing this, we will gain allies and funds. In June, we will bring about 500 Japanese students centered around Gwangju to show them around. Even if they spend just 150,000 won, that will bring in about 75 million won. Converted to dollars, that’s about 300,000 dollars, right? This shows how immense the money coming into Korea is.

Our wish
People from Jeollanam-do, raise your hands. If Japan doesn’t work, we will turn the world upside down. Therefore, if we mobilize 10,000 people in Gwangju, the governor of Jeollanam-do will have no choice but to mobilize everyone. Then we will focus on Gyeongsang-do. What will we do? Our business units will be organized centered around our principles, and everyone will be dispersed to evangelize and conduct business everywhere. If that happens, before long, I will earn more money in Korea than anyone else. At that time, I will give you whatever you want. (laughter)

Knowing this, if we manage to organize based on the foundation we currently have and proceed according to this plan, the foundation of our Unification Church will be established in Asia. Do you understand? "Yes." If this happens, a foundation will be created in the not-so-distant future that allows the teacher to say, "Come quickly," no matter what airplane he takes. Do you support this or oppose it? "I support it." There are six people related to this, including the Japanese Kubo family, and we need to lay the foundation so that they can freely travel by airplane. They should be able to come and go several times a day.

So will you follow the teacher and live as the teacher says, or will you live as you please? "I will live as the teacher says." Then you must listen well to the teacher. Young people here, will you listen to the teacher or not? "I will listen." Raise your hand if you won’t listen. Then raise your hand if you will listen well to the teacher. You have no choice but to listen…. You have been reborn as sons and daughters, so what can you do! Now that a lot of time has passed, we had a great feast for the 700 couples today. We didn’t eat, but we feel satisfied, right? "Yes." Did you think about food during this time, or not? "I didn’t." Then that means I spoke seriously and interestingly, right? "Yes." I feel good too! (laughter) 

Now, let’s sing the song of unification. I thought a lot about Jeongju today…. Let’s achieve unification! Do you understand? "Yes." When 600,000 troops are armed with the Unification Church ideology, we will be able to drive out the communists as easily as pulling fish out of a dry puddle. Do you understand? 

The path of restoration that families must take
The 1970s can be seen as a period when our Unification Church enters the completion stage of growth as a denomination. Why is that? It is because we have formed a tribal type centered around blessed families. Blessed families have the responsibility to restore their tribes.

Now is the time for families to indemnify.
Until now, it was an era of restoring families centered around the teacher. Therefore, in the 1960s, we went through a seven-year course for individual perfection. Now, in the 1970s, we must go through a seven-year course for family perfection. You still have a seven-year course left.

For you, the 1960s were a period of personal indemnity. Even if you had a family, it was a period of personal indemnity. However, now that the second seven-year course has begun and we have entered the 1970s, a path has finally opened for you to rise centered around your families.

The teacher is seven years ahead of you. Therefore, when the teacher stands in the position of the parents at the completion stage, it will be time for you to also start toward completion. This is the first seven-year course of the denomination.

So what is the first seven-year course? It is the time for your families to indemnify. Since families have not yet reached the completion stage, this is the course of indemnity for families to rise to the completion stage. You must not skip this seven-year course. Everyone must go through it.

However, since this path requires children to go together with their parents, if the parents do not take responsibility, they will have to indemnify together with their children. Adam and Eve fell at the completion stage of growth, so they could not establish a son-in-law expectation with Cain and Abel centered on God. Therefore, you must rise up from the completion stage of growth to restore. You must establish children of faith as a condition for this restoration. Even so, because they cannot be direct children of God, after being blessed, they must give birth to their direct children and establish a restored son-in-law expectation. This is how you will go through the first seven-year course.

Then what is the second seven-year course? It is the period of establishing the tradition of global families. The first seven-year course was the time to determine the center of global families, and during the second seven-year course, the patriarchs will take their positions on that expectation of families. Therefore, the second seven-year course is the time when families must bear the cross.

Then for whom must that cross be borne? It is not for the teacher. The teacher bore the cross for the nation and the world. Likewise, you must bear the cross for the nation and the world. The hopes of the parents and the hopes of the children must be the same.

Now families must indemnify. If conditions for Satan's accusation remain in the family, they cannot cross the path to completion. Therefore, until now, we have sent out evangelists from the position of individuals, but this time, we are sending you out to evangelize from the position of representing your families. You are being sent out to represent your families.

So who should go out first? Since this is a restoration course, women should go out first. Who should suffer first? Women should suffer first. The seven-year course was the period for mothers to indemnify. It was the period for raising one mother. Isn’t that right? Likewise, the reason we are sending your wives forward is that you must follow the path the teacher has taken.

How should you go on that path? You must go on the path of indemnity and restoration. The mistakes made by Eve must be restored by the mother. We must go back and gather what we have sown in the Unification Church until now. That is why this time, I commanded all blessed family wives to go back to the places they previously evangelized. I did not tell the men to go out. Do you understand?

However, the wife must be united in heart with her husband. She must be a wife who can lead her husband’s heart entirely. In other words, she must make her husband a sacrificial offering. Do you understand? You must understand that. To do this, you must sincerely report to your husband. Thus, the husband and wife must become one in heart. In this way, even if the mother goes out to evangelize alone from home, the husband and children must unite and joyfully welcome the mother who returns victorious. Otherwise, on this earth…
The conditions for the return of the fallen sons and daughters of the sun are not established. This is why we are doing this work to indemnify and restore it. 

You need to know what time it is now. You must understand what kind of time this is in the providential sense while engaging in such activities. Thus, the second seven-year course begins from the places where you went out to evangelize. The teacher combines the mistakes made by Adam, the mistakes made by Jesus, and his own mission to fulfill the third mission. This applies to you as well. The areas where you went out to evangelize are connected to you, so you must take responsibility for those places. This time, you are being asked to take full responsibility and come back. Do you understand? "Yes."

Invest your material, body, and heart. 
What could not be accomplished in the first seven-year course must be indemnified and restored in the second seven-year course. This time, husbands must also take responsibility. That is why this is the era of indemnification centered on families. You need to understand this. Among you, blessed families, raise your hands. Those who did not go out to evangelize this time, put your hands down. More than two-thirds must go out. Why is that? Because you must surpass the level of rebirth and growth. 

Look at this. Last summer, the teacher commanded us to pray with a special heart and announced that all blessed families would march forward. If everyone had gone out then, we would not have had a difficult path left for us. If you make mistakes, the teacher has to take responsibility for that alone. Until he cuts off all ties with you, he cannot do otherwise. That is how the law of indemnity works. However, if you take responsibility from now on, the Unification Church will survive. This cannot be denied. That is why it has come to the time since last year to bring forth forgiveness.

In the past, those who were considered prominent in society all opposed the Unification Church. However, the teacher did not regard them as enemies. What did they know back then? I hope for the day when they can come to kneel down on their own until this day. When that happens, the era of the Unification Church will come. 

In that regard, the 1970s is the era of the Unification Church. Therefore, it must be revealed nationally. Furthermore, it must be revealed in Asia. The recent Asian Victory Conference held in Korea was to reveal us to the outside world. It is to introduce the Unification Church in Korea. From here, the path to unification begins to open. Do you understand? 

From now on, I plan to do a lot of such work globally. Everyone needs to cooperate with that. So how will you cooperate? You must cooperate with your material, body, and heart. Material represents rebirth, body represents growth, and heart represents completion. You must invest all of this and cooperate. If you cooperate in this work, everything the teacher has received will be returned to you. As the times change, you will receive back according to how much you have cooperated. 

We Unification Church members have nothing. That is why until the 1970s, I have been working with the mindset of preparing a foundation for you, centering on the Sutaek-ri factory. Do you understand what I mean? That is why the teacher has been working hard to pave the way for you to be able to cooperate economically and with your body and heart since the 1970s. 

Once we surpass the 1970s, families will be freed from difficult economic circumstances. Do you understand? "Yes." However, you must not expect sympathy from the teacher. You must cooperate with the teacher using your material, body, and heart. You must do that. Why is that? Because when looking at the history of restoration centered on God, there is the era of offerings, the era of sons, and the era of parents. This can be seen as the era of rebirth, growth, and completion in terms of forms. 

When seen from the perspective of the teacher, you are in the position of children. You yourself are in the position of offerings like material. Then what is your body? It is the substantial offering, just like Jesus’ physical body was an offering. Then your heart must be united centered on the parents. This is eternal truth. If you do that, the world will naturally be restored. From there, heaven will unfold. The principle is that way. Do you understand? "Yes." 

Women need to understand this well. Then what do all women possess? Whose is it? It is God's. The bodies of women are God's, and their hearts are God's. They fell because the sun did not decide this. Is that not so? They did not know this... 

Therefore, in the Unification Church, women are central. So they have come out, putting in their sincerity without their husbands knowing. They have taught this way. When you know, everything is like this. 

Now, during the second seven-year course, you must bear the cross in your families. Before 1960, it was an era for individuals, and from 1960 onwards, it was an era starting from families. Now, we must establish a liberated nation by completely forming families, and for that, we must be completely united. But if we are fighting and hitting each other, can restoration happen? 

So, will you go out to evangelize again this summer, or not? "I will go out." If you don't want to go out, then stop. There is nothing more frightening than not sending you out. 

In the third seven-year course, men will also be sent out. Men must follow women. Originally, if all of you had gone out at once, there would have been no need for such games. But since that did not happen, men must follow. Men, will you follow? Will you not follow? "I will follow." Are you going to follow in a silly way? (Laughter) But it cannot be helped. 

Therefore, if women cannot sleep at night, men must not sleep at night either. That is how it should be. That is the subject. It is the same as how God puts in sincerity from the heavenly throne. It is the same as how Jesus put in sincerity on earth. Everything must be done on earth. Therefore, it is a problem to unfold the history of the Second Coming centered on the Unification Church on earth. You must take responsibility for this work. That is why it is even harder than the time of Jesus. Do you understand? You must prepare for three hundred sixty-five days and put in sincerity and offer it all to God. 

Is 1974 the year the second seven-year course ends? This year is the third year of the seven-year course and the last year of the three-year course. Originally, that three-year course was until June of this year. 

You must register centered on your families. But everyone, you have not registered yet, right? A frightening time will come. I will not explain it specifically. If the day comes, you must cut it off. That is the principle law. 

Looking at this, doing things centered on oneself is all unnecessary. However, today, both the nation and the world, as well as religions, all of humanity is living centered on individuals. We must have a new heart and raise the world with our strength. We must put in sincerity for the day we can do that. You must not fall down in the midst of a typhoon. Your families must do that. Do you understand? 

Families must support the church. No matter how big the Unification Church is and how great the Unification Church ideology is, it cannot be thought of without the ideal family ideology. However, since such expectations have not yet been fulfilled, your families must solidify this. Therefore, you must fight to establish a familial foundation that Satan cannot sever. In other words, you must take on the 5 percent responsibility that must be indemnified and restored at the family level. This responsibility must be completed by 1974, when the second seven-year course ends. Do you understand? 

The origin of happiness 
<Summary of the words> The happiness of a husband means he has a wife to whom he can give everything, and the happiness of parents means they have children to whom they can give everything. Because when you give completely, you can receive completely. 

When giving love to your partner and children, it should not just stay with them but should extend to the world. 

Adulterous love leads to ruin. 

A husband hopes his wife becomes a global wife, and a wife hopes her husband becomes a global person. That is because humans are global beings. 

Happiness must have factors that can last forever. God must have a counterpart to whom He can infinitely give to be happy. One cannot be happy alone. 

Those who only seek self-satisfaction will perish. A patriot is someone who lives for their country, a great person is someone who lives with global ambition, and a sage is someone who lives for heaven and earth. 

In the flat world, the nation represents heaven. Until now, the history of each nation has been a history that has pursued the ideological world. That is because ideology is global. 

There are not many intellectuals who have died as patriots. Rather, ignorant people have stood in the ranks of patriots. No matter how much someone has lived for their country, if they die without leaving a last will for their country, they cannot become a loyal subject. 

Union and unification are long-lasting. The question is how long happiness can last. 

What lasts forever is love, not doctrine. If you only choose those you want to love and love them, it will not last long. That is why Jesus showed compassion. Try giving. There is no way to perish by giving. Evangelism should not be done by choosing targets. You must evangelize with a heart that treats everyone equally. 

There has never been a nation that boasts of a thousand years of history as a nation that invaded others. 

If you keep yourself as you are, you cannot become leaven. You must change. You must become a being that can give. 

Do not try to make friends with money. Plant unforgettable affection. 

<Picture:028337.jpg>
Families must have a global nature. Heaven cannot be achieved without families. Also, there must be love. Love is inherited. If given wrongly, it leads to ruin. *
